<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column4715_75339f-11"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-large-font-size">Hey, I&#8217;m Whitney!</h2>

<p style="line-height:1.5">I&#8217;m on a DIY mission to empower ANYONE to get crafting, decorating, building, and Cricut-ing! I love all things home decor, power tools, and a long walk down the clearance aisle.</p>

<p style="line-height:1.5">Here you&#8217;ll find easy-to-follow tips, tricks, and DIY tutorials, including beginner-friendly Cricut DIYs. C&#8217;mon and join the Whiskey Craft Buddies to DIY along with us!</p>
